We present an integrative framework that emphasizes socioeconomic factors, health status, social context, and psychological factors to explain why some people fully retired after career exit, some participated in bridge jobs, while others unsuccessfully searched for one.\nDESIGN AND METHODS: Using Dutch panel data for 1,221 retirees, we estimated a multinomial logit model to explain participation in, and unsuccessful searches for, bridge employment.\nRESULTS: About 1 in 4 retirees participated in bridge employment after retirement, while 7% searched unsuccessfully for such work. Employment","title-short":"🔤桥就业","URL":"https://www.taylorfrancis.com/books/9781134094998","editor":[{"family":"Alcover","given":"Carlos-María"},{"family":"Topa","given":"Gabriela"},{"family":"Parry","given":"Emma"},{"family":"Fraccaroli","given":"Franco"},{"family":"Depolo","given":"Marco"}],"accessed":{"date-parts":[["2022",5,4]]},"issued":{"date-parts":[["2014",4,16]]}}},{"id":10301,"uris":["http://zotero.org/users/9278983/items/ZJD4CQFY"],"itemData":{"id":10301,"type":"article-journal","abstract":"高阶因子模型本质上是一种特殊的双因子模型,应用中却常被当做双因子模型的竞争模型。已有研究以满足比例约束的双因子模型(此时等价于一个高阶因子模型)为真实测量模型产生模拟数据,比较了用双因子模型和高阶因子模型作为测量模型的预测效果。本文使用不满足比例约束的双因子模型(此时不与任何高阶因子模型等价)为真实测量模型产生模拟数据进行比较,所得结果与满足比例约束的双因子模型的结果有很大差别,双因子模型结构系数的相对偏差较小、检验力较高,但第Ⅰ类错误率略高。结论是,在比例约束条件成立时可以使用高阶因子模型,否则,从统计角度看,一般情况下使用双因子模型进行预测比较好。","container-title":"心理学报","DOI":"10/gjpr2h","ISSN":"0439-755X","issue":"3","language":"zh","page":"383-391","source":"CNKI","title":"预测视角下双因子模型与高阶因子模型的一般性模拟比较","volume":"51","author":[{"literal":"温忠麟"},{"literal":"汤丹丹"},{"literal":"顾红磊"}],"issued":{"date-parts":[["2019"]]}}},{"id":2093,"uris":["http://zotero.org/users/9278983/items/DRGICZJS"],"itemData":{"id":2093,"type":"article-journal","abstract":"PURPOSE OF THE STUDY: Empirical studies on the determinants of bridge employment have often neglected the fact that some retirees may be unsuccessful in finding a bridge job. We present an integrative framework that emphasizes socioeconomic factors, health status, social context, and psychological factors to explain why some people fully retired after career exit, some participated in bridge jobs, while others unsuccessfully searched for one.\nDESIGN AND METHODS: Using Dutch panel data for 1,221 retirees, we estimated a multinomial logit model to explain participation in, and unsuccessful searches for, bridge employment.\nRESULTS: About 1 in 4 retirees participated in bridge employment after retirement, while 7% searched unsuccessfully for such work. Particularly those who experienced involuntary career exit were found to have a higher probability of being unsuccessful at finding bridge employment.\nIMPLICATIONS: The current study provides evidence for the impact of the social context on postretirement work and suggests a cumulative disadvantage in the work domain in later life.","container-title":"The Gerontologist","DOI":"10.1093/geront/gnu182","ISSN":"1758-5341","issue":"4","journalAbbreviation":"Gerontologist","language":"en-US","note":"PMID: 26035893","page":"630-640","source":"PubMed","title":"Access to Bridge Employment: Who Finds and Who Does Not Find Work After Retirement?","title-short":"🔤获得桥梁就业:谁发现谁不退休后找到工作?","volume":"56","author":[{"family":"Dingemans","given":"Ellen"},{"family":"Henkens","given":"Kène"},{"family":"Solinge","given":"Hanna","dropping-particle":"van"}],"issued":{"date-parts":[["2016",8]]}}}],"schema":"https://github.com/citation-style-language/schema/raw/master/csl-citation.json"}

uris:["http://zotero.org/users/9278983/items/DRGICZJS"], itemData:{id:2093, type:"article-journal", abstract:"PURPOSE OF THE STUDY: Empirical studies on the determinants of bridge employment have often neglected the fact that some retirees may be unsuccessful in finding a bridge job. We present an integrative framework that emphasizes socioeconomic factors, health status, social context, and psychological factors to explain why some people fully retired after career exit, some participated in bridge jobs, while others unsuccessfully searched for one.\nDESIGN AND METHODS: Using Dutch panel data for 1,221 retirees, we estimated a multinomial logit model to explain participation in, and unsuccessful searches for, bridge employment.\nRESULTS: About 1 in 4 retirees participated in bridge employment after retirement, while 7% searched unsuccessfully for such work. Particularly those who experienced involuntary career exit were found to have a higher probability of being unsuccessful at finding bridge employment.\nIMPLICATIONS: The current study provides evidence for the impact of the social context on postretirement work and suggests a cumulative disadvantage in the work domain in later life.", 'container-title':"The Gerontologist", DOI:"10.1093/geront/gnu182", ISSN:"1758-5341", issue:"4", journalAbbreviation:"Gerontologist", language:"en-US", note:"PMID: 26035893", page:"630-640", source:"PubMed", title:"Access to Bridge Employment: Who Finds and Who Does Not Find Work After Retirement?", 'title-short':"\uD83D\uDD24\u83B7\u5F97\u6865\u6881\u5C31\u4E1A:\u8C01\u53D1\u73B0\u8C01\u4E0D\u9000\u4F11\u540E\u627E\u5230\u5DE5\u4F5C?", volume:"56", author:[{family:"Dingemans", given:"Ellen"}, {family:"Henkens", given:"K\xE8ne"}, {family:"Solinge", given:"Hanna", 'dropping-particle':"van"}], issued:{'date-parts':[["2016", 8]]}}}], schema:"https://github.com/citation-style-language/schema/raw/master/csl-citation.json"}), [], []
